; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; SCHEDULER / TASK TABLE — COMPLETE 59-ENTRY MAP
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; The ECU runs a periodic task dispatcher from a scheduler table.
;
;   0x00E628:  sched_table_main     - Scheduler table, entry -> 0x04A94C
;   0x04A94C:  sched_periodic_dispatch  - Per-tick dispatcher, calls 59 tasks
;   0x04AD40:  task_table           - 59-entry periodic task pointer table
;              Each entry = 4-byte function pointer (big-endian)
;              Terminator = 0xFFFF8322 @ 0x04AE2C
;
; ─── TASK CATEGORIES ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   TIMING / PER-CYLINDER COMPENSATION (Tasks 0, 29)
;     Compute per-cylinder timing adjustments using RPM, MAF, and ECT inputs.
;     Reference calibration tables: Timing Comp Max RPM (0xD2D98),
;     Timing Comp Min Load (0xD2D9C), Timing Comp Min ECT (0xD2DA0).
;
;   KNOCK DETECTION & PROCESSING (Tasks 2, 5, 6, 7, 9, 11, 12, 23, 27, 42)
;     Read KNOCK_FLAG (0xFFFF81BA), KNOCK_BANK_FLAG (0xFFFF81BB).
;     Tasks 2/5/6/7 set GBR for per-cylinder knock window processing.
;     Task 11 is the main knock flag consumer — reads flag+bank, dispatches.
;     Task 12 post-processes knock data, references knock GBR base (0xFFFF80FC).
;     Task 42 combines knock with IAM (0xFFFF3234) for timing comp B decision.
;     Task 23 reads knock flag with cylinder index tracking (0xFFFF8294).
;     Task 27 reads knock flag with timing correction output (0xFFFF8268).
;
;   FLKC — FINE LEARNING KNOCK CORRECTION (Tasks 16, 17, 18, 19, 24, 25, 26, 28)
;     Adaptive knock correction with two response speeds:
;     Task 18 = flkc_path_J: fast-response (single-event retard)
;     Task 25 = flkc_paths_FG: sustained-knock (multi-condition retard)
;     Tasks 16/17 = FLKC pre-processing (read FLKC_BASE_STEP, IAM, KNOCK_FLAG)
;     Task 19 = FLKC post-processing (Advance Multiplier application)
;     Task 24/26 = FLKC output staging (write flkc_output_table 0xFFFF3360)
;     Task 28 = FLKC recovery (advance recovery step tables 0xD2EEC-0xD2F08)
;     Reference: Advance Multiplier Initial (0xD2EE0), Step (0xD2EE4)
;
;   KNOCK WINDOW / THRESHOLD SETUP (Tasks 3, 4, 8, 10, 13, 14, 15, 20, 21, 22)
;     Configure knock detection parameters per operating condition.
;     Tasks 3/4 set GBR for knock threshold tables, reference Feedback
;       Correction Min Load (0xD2DA4), knock sensitivity calibration.
;     Task 8 reads IAM + RPM for knock window setup, references 0xD2E1C-0xD2E2C.
;     Task 10 is a large multi-input task: RPM, MAF, scheduler status,
;       multiple RAM flags — likely the master knock configuration dispatcher.
;     Tasks 13/15 reference Rough Correction Min KC Advance (0xD2EDC) —
;       compute rough correction range for knock learning.
;     Task 14 reads knock threshold calibration (0xD2DEC-0xD2E04) — 8 params.
;     Tasks 20/21 set GBR, reference IAM — knock window per-cylinder updates.
;     Task 22 sets GBR, references cylinder index (0xFFFF8298) — per-cyl config.
;
;   KNOCK → TIMING FEEDBACK (Task 1)
;     Post-knock timing adjustment. References RAM 0xFFFF8204/8214/8218/821C
;     (knock correction state) and calibration 0xD299B. Uses FPU.
;
;   TIMING BLEND / MAP SWITCHING (Tasks 31, 32)
;     Task 31: Timing Blend ratio computation.
;       Refs: Timing Blend Ratio Floor (0xD2B18), Ceiling (0xD2B1C).
;     Task 32: Timing Blend application with RPM limiting.
;       Refs: Timing Blend Min Ratio (0xD2B10), RPM Limit (0xD2B14).
;
;   IGNITION TIMING CALCULATION (Tasks 30, 33, 34, 35, 36, 37)
;     Core timing computation pipeline — most reference RPM + MAF + ECT.
;     Task 30 (0x3FCA2): Large function, reads RPM, MAF, ECT, vehicle speed,
;       engine load, atmospheric pressure — likely base timing table lookup.
;       Sets GBR, calls sub 0x40314. References 14+ RAM variables.
;     Task 33 (0x40918): Multi-phase GBR setup, many GBR writes (+0x12 thru
;       +0x35) — initializes timing correction workspace. Calls 3 subroutines.
;     Task 34 (0x40516): Reads throttle position (0xFFFF65C0), MAF voltage
;       (0xFFFF6630/663C), injector data (0xFFFF895C) — timing compensation
;       based on fueling/throttle state.
;     Task 35 (0x418AC): References calibration near 0xD2C04, reads
;       timing state RAM (0xFFFF798C, 0xFFFF801C) — timing correction stage.
;     Task 36 (0x415B8): Reads RPM, MAF, throttle, fuel rate — applies
;       per-condition timing adjustments. Sets GBR.
;     Task 37 (0x419BA): RPM/MAF-based timing lookup with 3 calibration
;       references (0xD2C18-0xD2C20) and 3 BSR calls — multi-axis timing.
;
;   IGNITION OUTPUT / DWELL (Tasks 38, 39, 40, 41, 43, 44, 45, 46, 47, 48)
;     Final ignition timing and injector pulse width processing.
;     Task 38 (0x42A78): RPM + MAF + throttle → timing output.
;       Refs: calibration 0xD2CB0-0xD2CB8 (3 tables). Uses RPM, injector RAM.
;     Task 39 (0x42B90): MAF-based correction with RAM 0xFFFF320C reference.
;     Tasks 40/41 (0x42D20/0x42D54): Pair — both read 0xFFFF320C + MAF,
;       reference same calibration (0xD2CC8/0xD2CCC). Task 41 calls sub 0x42E6A.
;     Task 42 (0x42F48): IAM-gated timing comp. Knock flag + IAM → decide
;       if Timing Comp B (IAT) activates. Ref: IAM Activation (0xD2CF4).
;     Task 43 (0x4322A): Timing output with load (0xFFFF6254) reference.
;     Tasks 44/45 (0x4317A/0x431B0): RPM + MAF timing lookup pair.
;       Both ref same calibration (0xD2D10) and descriptors (0xADFC0).
;     Task 46 (0x43368): References MAF voltage (0xFFFF6650/6654), manifold
;       pressure (0xFFFF6790), boost (0xFFFF6810). Calls low_pw_table_proc.
;       Likely injector dead-time or manifold-pressure timing compensation.
;     Task 47 (0x43464): Map Switching integration — references Map Switch
;       Torque Ratio (0xD2A0C), IAT Threshold (0xD2A1C), plus Low PW
;       Injector Comp thresholds (0xD2D20-0xD2D2C). Calls low_pw_table_proc.
;     Task 48 (0x4359C): Final timing/injector output — reads throttle,
;       MAF, boost pressure (0xFFFF6812). 4 JSR calls + BSR to 0x436B6.
;
;   IGNITION BASE TIMING / ADVANCE (Tasks 49, 50)
;     Task 49 (0x3F00C): Comprehensive timing input — reads RPM, MAF, load,
;       throttle, fuel rate, atmospheric pressure. 16+ RAM refs. Sets GBR.
;       Likely the main base timing advance lookup function.
;     Task 50 (0x3F368): RPM + MAF + timing blend integration. References
;       cl_global_enable (0xFFFF8F24), scheduler status. Sets GBR.
;       Applies timing blend results to final advance value.
;
;   BOOST / WASTEGATE CONTROL (Tasks 51, 52)
;     Task 51 (0x54852): Reads throttle (0xFFFF65C0), fuel rate, MAF voltage
;       (0xFFFF6640/6644). Refs: Coolant Temp tables (0xD6718-0xD6724).
;       Sets GBR, writes +0x80. Boost target / wastegate duty calculation.
;     Task 52 (0x549FA): MAF-based boost correction. Refs: 0xD6748 calibration.
;       Calls utility 0x22F92. Boost feedback / trim adjustment.
;
;   DIAGNOSTICS / DTC (Tasks 53, 55, 58)
;     Task 53 (0x602DC): Reads diagnostic state RAM (0xFFFF9084/9088/9090).
;       Calibration ref 0xD9A4C. Calls 2 subroutines. Diagnostic monitor.
;     Task 55 (0x900B4): Manifold Pressure Sensor diagnostics.
;       Refs: MPS calibration (0xD8A51/0xD8AB8/0xD8B14), MAF sensor (0xD8BC4).
;       Reads atmospheric data (0xFFFFABF4). Sensor validation/CEL logic.
;     Task 58 (0x6F0B8): MAF sensor diagnostics.
;       Refs: MAF/MPS calibration (0xD8B14/0xD8B18). Reads MAF + ATM data.
;       Sensor cross-check / rationality test.
;
;   IDLE / SPEED CONTROL (Task 54)
;     Task 54 (0x4BC20): Sets GBR. References throttle-related RAM
;       (0xFFFF65A9/65D2) and calibration 0xD6011/0xD6012. No FPU.
;       Multiple GBR reads/writes — likely idle speed controller state machine.
;
;   EVAP / PURGE CONTROL (Task 56)
;     Task 56 (0x66580): No FPU, no MAF/RPM references. Reads RAM 0xFFFF2368/
;       236C. Calls 2 subroutines (0x66D20, 0x66DEC). Likely EVAP purge
;       solenoid control or canister purge logic.
;
;   EGR / EMISSIONS (Task 57)
;     Task 57 (0x758CA): Sets GBR, reads MAF. Calibration ref 0xC4755
;       (primary calibration region). References high-address RAM (0xFFFFA198/
;       A224). Calls multiple utility functions. Emissions-related control.
;
; ─── COMPLETE TASK TABLE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
;
;  Idx  TblAddr   FuncAddr    Category                    Notes
;  ───  ───────   ────────    ────────                    ─────

;
; ─── EXECUTION ORDER OBSERVATIONS ──────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   The task table execution order reflects a deliberate pipeline:
;
;   1. INPUTS & SETUP     [0-10]  Per-cylinder timing comp, knock window
;                                  config, knock detection processing
;   2. KNOCK RESPONSE     [11-15] Knock flag consumption, post-processing,
;                                  rough correction range computation
;   3. FLKC PIPELINE      [16-28] FLKC pre-process → fast path (J) →
;                                  sustained path (F/G) → output → recovery
;   4. TIMING PIPELINE    [29-48] Per-cyl comp → base lookup → blend →
;                                  workspace init → corrections → final output
;   5. BASE ADVANCE       [49-50] Master base timing + blend integration
;   6. ACTUATORS & DIAG   [51-58] Boost/WG, diagnostics, idle, EVAP, EGR

; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; SHARED SUBROUTINE CATALOG (Top ~70 by cross-reference count)
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; Found via BSR/JSR call-target analysis of the full 1MB ROM. These are the
; most-called functions that appear across all subsystems. Naming them is the
; single highest-leverage action for future disassembly — every function you
; trace will reference several of these.
;
; ─── ALREADY LABELED (Table Processor Library, 0xBE608-0xBED98) ───────────
;   See ImportAE5L600L.java for the complete table processor library:
;   uint8_pack (1000), table_desc_1d_float (524), uint8_unpack (425),
;   uint16_pack (416), uint16_unpack (270), float_max (261), float_min (227),
;   table_desc_2d_typed (170), float_deadband_check (154), float_abs_diff (152),
;   float_lerp (147), float_safe_div (145), plus all interp_1d/2d variants.
;
; ─── INTEGER ARITHMETIC ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0xBE554: uint16_add_sat          (685 calls)
;     r0 = min(r4 + r5, 0xFFFF). Saturating 16-bit add.
;     Appears in virtually every calibration write path.
;
;   0xBE53C: uint8_add_sat           (461 calls)
;     r0 = min(r4 + r5, 0xFF). Saturating 8-bit add with carry check.
;     Used by all 8-bit calibration table outputs.
;
; ─── DESCRIPTOR / TABLE READ (NaN-safe) ───────────────────────────────────
;
;   0xBDBCC: desc_read_float_safe    (309 calls)
;     Reads float from descriptor pointer r4 with NaN-check (fcmp/eq self).
;     Calls interrupt_priority_set(16) + interrupt_restore for atomicity.
;     THE most important unlabeled function in the ROM — appears in every
;     calibration read path involving floating-point outputs.
;
;   0xBDCB6: desc_read_int_safe      (120 calls)
;     Integer variant of desc_read_float_safe. Same atomic read pattern.
;
; ─── INTERRUPT PRIORITY CONTROL ───────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0x0317C: interrupt_priority_set   (298 calls)
;     Sets SR interrupt mask to level r4 (0-15). Returns old SR in r0.
;     Every descriptor/table read calls this first for data consistency.
;
;   0x03190: interrupt_restore        (181 calls)
;     Restores SR interrupt mask from r4. Paired with interrupt_priority_set.
;     May call 0x3664 via indirect dispatch if flag at FFFF1288+0x18 is set.
;
; ─── CRITICAL SECTION (lightweight SR-mask wrappers) ──────────────────────
;
;   0xBE81C: critical_section_enter   (235 calls)
;     Saves SR, masks interrupt level from 0xF0, stores old priority at @r4.
;
;   0xBE82C: critical_section_exit    (236 calls)
;     Restores SR from r4. Just: rts + ldc r4,sr. Paired with enter.
;
; ─── FLOAT RANGE / CLAMP ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0xBE56C: float_clamp_range        (218 calls)
;     Clamps fr4 to [fr6..fr5]. Returns in fr0.
;     Core range limiter for every calibration output.
;
; ─── AXIS INTERPOLATION PRIMITIVES ────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0xBE5D8: axis_frac_to_uint16      (147 calls)
;     Converts float axis value to uint16 index+fraction for table lookup.
;     Computes (value-base)/range, ftrc→int, clamps [0, 0xFFFF].
;
;   0xBE5A8: axis_frac_to_uint8       (113 calls)
;     Same as above, clamps to [0, 0xFF].
;
;   0xBE598: fmac_interp_uint16       (145 calls)
;     Converts uint16 fraction r4 to float, fmac blend: fr0 = fr4 + fr3*(fr5-fr4).
;     Core 1D interpolation for uint16-indexed tables.
;
;   0xBE588: fmac_interp_uint8         (31 calls)
;     Same for uint8-indexed tables.
;
; ─── CONTEXT SAVE (ISR entry) ─────────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0x02B8C: isr_context_save         (118 calls)
;     Full register save: r2-r7, fr0-fr10, FPUL, PR → stack.
;     Increments FFFF1288+8 counter. Returns restore-routine address in r0.
;     Every interrupt handler entry calls this.
;
; ─── STATUS CHECK HELPERS (single-byte RAM flag reads) ────────────────────
;
;   0x22F92: check_cl_active           (111 calls) → FFFF65F6
;   0x22CF4: check_engine_running      (100 calls) → FFFF65C5
;   0x2F8EA: check_transient_flag       (65 calls) → FFFF726C
;   0x3AB20: check_engine_status        (35 calls) → FFFF7C68
;
;   Each reads a single byte from RAM, returns T-bit = (value==1).
;   Used as gate checks throughout fuel, timing, and diagnostic code.
;
; ─── DTC FRAMEWORK ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0x9EDEC: dtc_set_code             (186 calls) — Set DTC by index r4
;   0x9ED90: dtc_clear_code           (140 calls) — Clear DTC by index r4
;   0x9CFEE: dtc_scan_loop             (48 calls) — Iterate all DTCs
;   0x98686: dtc_status_check           (14 calls) — Check specific fault state
;   0x9D052: dtc_counter_update         (14 calls) — Increment maturation counter
;   0x9DD78: dtc_vector_table           (17 calls) — Handler dispatch table
;   0x9CABE: dtc_freeze_frame           (11 calls) — Capture freeze frame data
;   0x9884E: dtc_monitor_helper         (12 calls) — Shared monitor logic
;   0x98832: dtc_monitor_gate           (10 calls) — Monitor enable conditions
;   0x9DCEA: dtc_history_update         (10 calls) — Write fault history
;
;   DTC table starts at 0x9A770 (93 OBD-II codes). Gate: FFFFB71C enable
;   + FFFF36F4 processing flag.
;
; ─── DIAGNOSTIC / SENSOR VALIDATION ──────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0x582D2: diag_wrapper_set          (108 calls) — Wrapper for 0xA6728
;   0x582AC: diag_check_status         (100 calls) — Read FFFF36F0 mode byte
;   0x582E0: diag_read_pack_2val        (43 calls) — Pack 2 values atomically
;   0x584C8: diag_check_enable_B        (59 calls) → FFFFAE09
;   0x584BE: diag_check_enable_A        (43 calls) → FFFFAE08
;
; ─── SCHEDULER / TIMER ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0x0E6E4: sched_event_post           (73 calls) — Post event (atomic)
;   0x0E6C4: sched_event_clear          (11 calls) — Clear event flag
;   0x0E794: sched_timer_dispatch         (8 calls) — Timer callback manager
;
; ─── PERIPHERAL I/O WRAPPERS ─────────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0x06BC4: io_write_word_atomic       (35 calls)
;   0x06BF0: io_write_2word_atomic      (31 calls)
;   0x06828: io_read_word_atomic        (15 calls)
;   0x06884: io_read_2word_atomic       (20 calls)
;   0x067A6: io_sched_event_atomic      (26 calls)
;   0x067DC: io_sched_event_atomic_2    (21 calls)
;
;   All use critical_section_enter/exit for atomicity.
;
; ─── COMMUNICATION PROTOCOL ──────────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0x58318: comms_pack_response        (57 calls)
;   0x58404: comms_pack_response_B      (49 calls)
;
;   Build multi-byte diagnostic responses (KWP2000/CAN).
;   Call interrupt_priority_set, uint16_pack, uint8_pack, interrupt_restore.
;
; ─── DESCRIPTOR TABLE WALKER ──────────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0x0DCE4: desc_table_walk            (37 calls)
;     Walks multi-entry calibration descriptors via lookup table at 0x11B98.
;     Iterates entries with shift+add addressing loop.
;
;   0x06B5A: calc_table_offset          (53 calls)
;     Computes calibration table addresses from base 0xC0080 + lookup
;     tables at 0x1190C/0x11914/0x1193C.
;
; ─── RAM CHANGE DETECTION ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0x0B9E0: ram_word_update            (44 calls)
;   0x0B99C: ram_word_update_B          (22 calls)
;   0x10800: event_notify               (15 calls)
;
;   Compare-and-write pattern: if word at @r14 changed, fire event_notify.
;
; ─── MISC HIGH-VALUE ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0x4E0B8: gbr_task_dispatcher        (40 calls) — GBR=0xFFFF83AB, 64B workspace
;   0x297A0: float_load_from_desc       (18 calls) — Float read from descriptor
;   0x297B0: float_load_from_desc_B     (16 calls) — Variant
;   0x299BC: float_store_to_ram         (14 calls) — Float write from descriptor
;   0x45EEA: knock_helper_leaf          (13 calls) — Leaf in knock pipeline
;   0x23E48: fuel_desc_reader           (15 calls) — PSE/fuel descriptor read
;   0x21D9A: cl_readiness_check         (12 calls) — CL readiness evaluation

;   0x117FC: hw_register_get            (13 calls) — Hardware register read

;   0xFFFF726C: transient_flag      — 1=transient condition (65 refs)
;   0xFFFF7C68: engine_status_flag  — 1=normal (35 refs, gates AFL)

;
; ─── CALIBRATION DESCRIPTOR FORMAT ───────────────────────────────────────
;   (Full scan in disassembly/descriptor_map.txt — 760 descriptors)
;
;   1D Descriptor (20 bytes):
;     +0x00: [0x00, axis_size, data_type, 0x00]
;     +0x04: axis_ptr  (ROM -> float32[axis_size])
;     +0x08: data_ptr  (ROM -> data[axis_size])
;     +0x0C: scale     (float32: physical = raw * scale + bias)
;     +0x10: bias      (float32)
;
;   2D Descriptor (28 bytes):
;     +0x00: [0x00, Y_size, 0x00, X_size]
;     +0x04: Y_axis_ptr (ROM -> float32[Y_size])
;     +0x08: X_axis_ptr (ROM -> float32[X_size])
;     +0x0C: data_ptr   (ROM -> data[Y_size * X_size])
;     +0x10: [data_type, 0, 0, 0]
;     +0x14: scale      (float32)
;     +0x18: bias       (float32)
;
;   Data types: 0x00=float32, 0x02=int8, 0x04=int16, 0x08=uint8, 0x0A=uint16
;   Discriminator: byte[3] == 0 -> 1D, byte[3] != 0 -> 2D
;   Found: 621 x 1D + 139 x 2D = 760 total
;
;   Axis classification (auto-named, see disassembly/named_descriptors.txt):
;     1D: ECT(258), RPM(79), Throttle(41), RPM_wide(27), Boost(26), Load(24)
;     2D: LoadxRPM(48), ThrottlexRPM(5), AtmPressurexRPM(4), VVTErrorxRPM(4)
;
; ─── DTC TABLE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
;   (Full decode in disassembly/dtc_table.txt — 93 entries, 91 identified)
;
;   Flag table:  0x9A770 (93 bytes, 0x01=enabled)
;   Struct table: 0x9A834 (93 x 20-byte entries)
;   Struct: [W0:class] [W1:monitor_id] [P-code] [W3:subtype] [params]
;
; ─── RAM ADDRESS MAP ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
;   (Full scan in disassembly/ram_map_raw.txt — 4,456 unique addresses)
;
;   Top addresses by reference count:

;     0xFFFF399E dtc_maturation    118 refs

; ─── SH7058 PERIPHERAL REGISTERS ─────────────────────────────────────────
;   14 on-chip register addresses referenced in ROM:
;     0xFFFF0000 STBCR     (9 refs) -- Standby/power control
;     0xFFFF0004 STBCR2    (2 refs) -- Module stop bits
;     0xFFFF1230 TIER_MTU0 (3 refs) -- Timer interrupt enable
;     0xFFFF12B8 SCI_TDR   (5 refs) -- Serial transmit data
;     0xFFFF12C8 SCI_SSR   (2 refs) -- Serial status
;
; ─── THUNK RESOLUTION ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
;   (Full: disassembly/thunk_resolution.txt, 359 lines)
;   378 mov.l+jmp thunks found. 64 resolve to known functions:
;     interrupt_restore    <- 15 thunks (tail-call from ISR handlers)
;     desc_read_float_safe <- 5+ thunks (descriptor read wrappers)
;
; ─── DESCRIPTOR-FUNCTION CROSS-REFERENCE ─────────────────────────────────
;   (Full: disassembly/desc_func_xref.txt, 1,495 lines)
;   Top functions by descriptor count:
;     afl_pipeline           61 desc  (most calibration-heavy subsystem)
;     task33_timing_ws_init  30 desc
;     PSE_code               22 desc
;     timing_knock           20 desc
;
; --- ROM REGION MAP -----------------------------------------------------------
;   (Full: disassembly/rom_region_map.txt, 3,194 lines)
;
;   Region distribution (1MB ROM):
;     Code:        444,928 bytes (42.4%)
;     Float data:  395,776 bytes (37.7%) -- calibration tables
;     ROM holes:   194,560 bytes (18.6%) -- 0xFF filled, patch space
;     Other:        13,312 bytes ( 1.3%)
;
;   PATCH-AVAILABLE ROM HOLES (190.9 KB total):
;     0x0DAE8C-0x0F8900  118.6 KB  PRIMARY (confirmed, used by MerpMod)

;     0x0FC004-0x0FFAF8   14.7 KB  TERTIARY (end of ROM)

; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; KNOCK DETECTION & FLKC (Fine Learning Knock Correction) ANALYSIS
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; Reverse-engineered from Ghidra SH-2 analysis of the knock correction system.
; Two GBR contexts: knock_detector uses GBR=0xFFFF80FC,
;                   flkc_paths_FG uses GBR=0xFFFF8290.
;
; ─── Functions ───────────────────────────────────────
;
;   0x043750:  knock_wrapper
;              Checks cylinder index R4 in {0,6,12,18} and counter < 4,
;              then BSR to knock_detector (0x043782).
;
;   0x043782:  knock_detector
;              Actual knock detection routine.  GBR = 0xFFFF80FC.
;              Writes KNOCK_FLAG [0xFFFF81BA] = 1 (knock) or 0 (no knock)
;              Writes KNOCK_BANK_FLAG [0xFFFF81BB] = bank index (0 or 1)
;
;   0x045BFE:  flkc_path_J  (task [18])
;              FLKC fast-response correction.
;              If KNOCK_FLAG != 0: FR13 -= base_step * 0.5
;              At stock: base_step=0.5, multiplier=0.5 -> retard = -0.25 steps.
;              ROM[0x045DD8] = 0x3F000000 = 0.5 (multiplier constant).
;              Fires every cycle knock is detected. No bank discrimination.
;
;   0x0463BA:  flkc_paths_FG  (task [25])
;              FLKC sustained-knock correction.  GBR = 0xFFFF8290.
;              Requires 7 conditions including knock flag, counter >= 90,
;              cylinder index match, and FP range checks.
;              Branches on KNOCK_BANK_FLAG:
;                bank != 1 -> PATH F: FR4 -= 1.01  (ROM[0xD2F50])
;                bank == 1 -> PATH F: FR4 -= 2.80  (ROM[0xD2F64])
;                early bail -> PATH G: FR4 -= 1.01  (ROM[0xD2F50])
;
; ─── ROM Constants (FLKC literal pool) ──────────────
;
;   0x045DD8:  PATH_J_HALFSTEP_MULT  = 0x3F000000 = 0.5
;              Path J multiplier. retard = RAM[0xFFFF323C] * 0.5 = 0.25 steps.
;              Change to 0x3F800000 (1.0) for full-step, 0x3F400000 (0.75) for 3/4.
;
;   0x0D2F40:  FLKC_FG_LIMIT_100   = 0x42C80000 = 100.0  (FR15 upper limit)
;   0x0D2F44:  tbl_d2f44_8p0       = 0x41000000 = 8.0
;   0x0D2F48:  tbl_d2f48_0p25      = 0x3E800000 = 0.25
;   0x0D2F4C:  tbl_d2f4c_n15       = 0xC1700000 = -15.0
;   0x0D2F50:  FLKC_RETARD_STEP    = 0x3F8147AE = 1.01  (Path F & G retard step)
;   0x0D2F54:  tbl_d2f54_0p35      = 0x3EB33333 = 0.35
;   0x0D2F58:  tbl_d2f58_0p35      = 0x3EB33333 = 0.35
;   0x0D2F5C:  tbl_d2f5c_1p40      = 0x3FB33333 = 1.40
;   0x0D2F60:  tbl_d2f60_1p40      = 0x3FB33333 = 1.40
;   0x0D2F64:  FLKC_RETARD_BANK1   = 0x40333333 = 2.80  (Path F bank-1 step)
;   0x0D2F68:  tbl_d2f68_2p80      = 0x40333333 = 2.80
;
; ─── RAM Variables ───────────────────────────────────
;
;   0xFFFF80FC:  knock_det_GBR_base    - GBR base for knock_detector
;   0xFFFF81BA:  KNOCK_FLAG            - 1=knock detected, 0=no knock (per cycle)
;   0xFFFF81BB:  KNOCK_BANK_FLAG       - Bank selector: 1=bank1, 0=bank0
;   0xFFFF81D9:  fn_043d68_output      - Written by task [12], NOT the knock flag
;   0xFFFF323C:  FLKC_BASE_STEP        - Base correction step (float), = 0.5 stock
;   0xFFFF8290:  flkc_fg_GBR_base      - GBR base for flkc_paths_FG
;   0xFFFF8294:  flkc_fg_counter       - Cycle counter, must be >= 90 for F/G
;   0xFFFF8298:  flkc_fg_cyl_index     - Current cylinder/bank index
;   0xFFFF829C:  flkc_fg_active        - Active flag; cleared on knock entry
;   0xFFFF829D:  flkc_fg_retard_done   - Set to 1 after retard applied
;   0xFFFF829E:  flkc_fg_enable        - Must == 1 to enter main logic
;   0xFFFF82A0:  flkc_fg_exit_flag     - Set to 1 at normal exit
;   0xFFFF82A1:  flkc_fg_bank_route    - Routes post-retard clamp fn call
;   0xFFFF82AA:  flkc_fg_prev_cyl      - Previous cylinder; must match for retard
;   0xFFFF8258:  flkc_fg_limit_FR15    - Loaded into FR15, compared vs 100.0
;   0xFFFF3234:  flkc_fg_ref_FR14      - Loaded into FR14 at entry
;   0xFFFF3244:  flkc_fg_R0_init       - Early R0 setup
;   0xFFFF3248:  flkc_fg_var_3248      - Read in setup
;   0xFFFF8233:  flkc_fg_flag_8233     - Byte flag checked during FP setup
;   0xFFFF7D18:  sched_status_R1       - Read at fn_0463ba entry
;   0xFFFF3360:  flkc_output_table     - Output (word array indexed by cylinder)
;   0xFFFF8EDC:  sched_disable_flag    - If != 0, entire dispatch is skipped

; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; FUELING ANALYSIS — FAILSAFE MAP BEHAVIOR
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; When IAM (Ignition Advance Multiplier) drops below the threshold at
; 'Primary Open Loop Fuel Map Switch (IAM)' @ 0xCC16C, the ECU switches
; from normal fuel maps to the Failsafe fuel map @ 0xD05C4.
;
; IAM Switch Thresholds @ 0xCC16C:
;   Threshold 1: IAM = 0.5000  (begin failsafe transition)
;   Threshold 2: IAM = 0.0500  (full failsafe)
;
; Normal Maps (KCA Low/High @ 0xD0244/0xD0404, Alternate @ 0xCFD30):
;   Max raw value = 0x2B (43) -> minimum AFR = 11.00
;
; Failsafe Map (@ 0xD05C4):
;   Max raw value = 0x46 (70) -> minimum AFR = 9.50
;   At 2000 RPM / 2.60 g/rev: raw = 0x3C (60)
;     AFR = 14.7 / (1 + 60 * 0.0078125) = 14.7 / 1.46875 = 10.01 ~ 10.02
;   This is the root cause of observed "10.02 AFR Final Fueling Base".

; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; POST START ENRICHMENT (PSE) TABLES
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; Code function at 0x30674-0x30A78.
; 26 ECU descriptor entries at 0xAC948-0xACB3F.
; 13 calibration tables + 2 Coolant Temperature axes.
;
; ─── Descriptor Format ───────────────────────────────
;   20-byte: [meta(4)][axis_ptr(4)][data_ptr(4)][scale_float(4)][pad(4)]
;   12-byte: [meta(4)][axis_ptr(4)][data_ptr(4)]  (no scale = direct value)
;   Meta 0x00100800 = 16 elements, uint16 storage.
;
; ─── Scale Factor Identification ─────────────────────
;   0x3B800000 = 0.00390625     -> Post_Start_Enrich_Decay1 (LSD Initial)
;   0x39800000 = 0.000244140625 -> Post_Start_Enrich_Decay  (HSD Initial Start)
;   0x35800000 = 9.5367e-7      -> Post_Start_Enrich_Decay2 (HSD Step Value)
;   0x3C000000 = 0.0078125      -> Post_Start_Enrich_Decay4 (LSD Delay Multiplier)
;   (no scale)                  -> Post_Start_Enrich_Decay3 (LSD Delay, direct)
;
; ─── CT Axes ─────────────────────────────────────────
;   0xCC624:  PSE_CT_Axis_1  - 16 float32, -40 to 110 deg F (used by 12 tables)
;   0xCC664:  PSE_CT_Axis_2  - 16 float32, -40 to 110 deg F (used by LSD Delay 2)
;
; ─── Descriptors at 0xAC948-0xACB3F ──────────────────
;   0xAC948:  PSE_Desc_LSD_Initial_1A       -> data 0xCD3A6, axis 0xCC624, Decay1
;   0xAC95C:  PSE_Desc_LSD_Initial_1B       -> data 0xCD3C6, axis 0xCC624, Decay1
;   0xAC970:  PSE_Desc_LSD_Initial_2A       -> data 0xCD3E6, axis 0xCC624, Decay1
;   0xAC984:  PSE_Desc_LSD_Initial_2B       -> data 0xCD406, axis 0xCC624, Decay1
;   0xAC998:  PSE_Desc_LSD_Delay_1          -> data 0xCD426, axis 0xCC624 (12-byte)
;   0xAC9A4:  PSE_Desc_HSD_InitStart_1A     -> data 0xCD446, axis 0xCC624, Decay
;   0xAC9B8:  PSE_Desc_HSD_InitStart_Zero1  -> data 0xCD466 (zeros)
;   0xAC9CC:  PSE_Desc_HSD_InitStart_Zero2  -> data 0xCD486 (zeros)
;   0xAC9E0:  PSE_Desc_HSD_InitStart_1B     -> data 0xCD4A6, axis 0xCC624, Decay
;   0xAC9F4:  PSE_Desc_HSD_InitStart_Zero3  -> data 0xCD4C6 (zeros)
;   0xACA08:  PSE_Desc_HSD_InitStart_2A     -> data 0xCD4E6, axis 0xCC624, Decay
;   0xACA1C:  PSE_Desc_HSD_InitStart_Zero4  -> data 0xCD506 (zeros)
;   0xACA30:  PSE_Desc_HSD_InitStart_Zero5  -> data 0xCD526 (zeros)
;   0xACA44:  PSE_Desc_HSD_InitStart_2B     -> data 0xCD546, axis 0xCC624, Decay
;   0xACA58:  PSE_Desc_HSD_InitStart_Zero6  -> data 0xCD566 (zeros)
;   0xACA6C:  PSE_Desc_LSD_Delay_2          -> data 0xCD586, axis 0xCC664 (12-byte)
;   0xACA78:  PSE_Desc_HSD_StepValue_1      -> data 0xCD5A6, axis 0xCC624, Decay2
;   0xACA8C:  PSE_Desc_HSD_StepValue_Zero1  -> data 0xCD5C6 (zeros)
;   0xACAA0:  PSE_Desc_HSD_StepValue_2      -> data 0xCD5E6, axis 0xCC624, Decay2
;   0xACAB4:  PSE_Desc_HSD_StepValue_Zero2  -> data 0xCD606 (zeros)
;   0xACAC8:  PSE_Desc_HSD_StepValue_Zero3  -> data 0xCD626 (zeros)
;   0xACADC:  PSE_Desc_HSD_StepValue_Zero4  -> data 0xCD646 (zeros)
;   0xACAF0:  PSE_Desc_LSD_DelayMult        -> data 0xCD666, axis 0xCC624, Decay4
;   0xACB04:  PSE_Desc_LSD_DelayMult_Zero   -> data 0xCD686 (zeros)
;   0xACB18:  PSE_Desc_HSD_InitStart_Extra1 -> data 0xCD6A6 (zeros)
;   0xACB2C:  PSE_Desc_HSD_InitStart_Extra2 -> data 0xCD6C6 (zeros)
;
; ─── Code Literal Pools ──────────────────────────────
;   0x30674:  LSD Initial group pointers
;             0x30674 -> 0xAC970 (LSD Init 2A)
;             0x30684 -> 0xAC984 (LSD Init 2B)
;             0x30688 -> 0xAC948 (LSD Init 1A)
;             0x3068C -> 0xAC95C (LSD Init 1B)
;   0x306CC:  LSD Delay 1 pointer -> 0xAC998
;   0x309EC:  HSD Initial Start group (10 pointers, 4 active + 6 zero)
;             0x30A04 -> 0xAC9A4 (HSD Init 1A)
;             0x30A10 -> 0xAC9E0 (HSD Init 1B)
;             0x30A0C -> 0xACA08 (HSD Init 2A)
;             0x30A18 -> 0xACA44 (HSD Init 2B)
;   0x30A3C:  LSD Delay 2 pointer -> 0xACA6C
;   0x30A4C:  LSD Delay Mult + extra HSD Init pointers
;   0x30A60:  HSD Step Value group (6 pointers, 2 active + 4 zero)
;             0x30A60 -> 0xACA78 (HSD Step 1)
;             0x30A6C -> 0xACAA0 (HSD Step 2)
;
; ─── Active PSE Data Tables ──────────────────────────
;   Address   Table Name                                     Scaling        Status
;   0xCD3A6   LSD Initial 1A  (16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC624)   Decay1         active
;   0xCD3C6   LSD Initial 1B  (16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC624)   Decay1         active
;   0xCD3E6   LSD Initial 2A  (16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC624)   Decay1         active
;   0xCD406   LSD Initial 2B  (16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC624)   Decay1         active
;   0xCD426   LSD Delay 1     (16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC624)   Decay3(direct) flat=38
;   0xCD446   HSD InitStart 1A(16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC624)   Decay          active
;   0xCD4A6   HSD InitStart 1B(16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC624)   Decay          active
;   0xCD4E6   HSD InitStart 2A(16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC624)   Decay          active
;   0xCD546   HSD InitStart 2B(16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC624)   Decay          active
;   0xCD586   LSD Delay 2     (16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC664)   Decay3(direct) all zeros
;   0xCD5A6   HSD StepValue 1 (16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC624)   Decay2         active
;   0xCD5E6   HSD StepValue 2 (16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC624)   Decay2         active
;   0xCD666   LSD DelayMult   (16 x uint16, CT @ 0xCC624)   Decay4         active
;
; NOTE: 32BITBASE.xml defines Decay3 and Decay4 as uint8, but this ROM stores uint16.

; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; TRANSIENT FUEL CONTROL — THREE INDEPENDENT SUBSYSTEMS
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
;
; The ECU uses three independent transient fuel compensation systems that
; operate on different input signals and combine additively in the final
; fuel correction accumulator (0x320AE):
;
;   1. TIP-IN ENRICHMENT — throttle-rate based (rising throttle only)
;   2. TAU (ALPHA TRANSIENT) — load-rate based (rising AND falling load)
;   3. OVERRUN FUEL CUTOFF — deceleration fuel cut with resume enrichment
;
; ─── Execution Order in Pipeline B ───────────────────
;   0x37186  fuel_transient_comp    — Tip-in/out transient compensation
;   0x37B68  fuel_injector_comp     — Injector compensation maps
;   0x39528  fuel_wot_enrich_calc   — WOT enrichment factor
;   0x3A222  fuel_per_cyl_trim      — Per-cylinder trim (4-cyl loop)
;   0x3BB6C  fuel_accel_enrich      — Acceleration enrichment
;   0x3CD34  fuel_warmup_enrich     — Warmup/cold-start enrichment
;   0x3EB8C  fuel_overrun_cutoff    — Deceleration fuel cut
;
; ─── How Tip-In and Tau Interact ─────────────────────
;   During a typical tip-in event:
;   1. Driver stabs throttle -> tip-in fires FIRST (throttle moves before load)
;      Adds IPW (ms) based on throttle angle change rate
;   2. As turbo spools -> Tau fires SECOND (load follows throttle with lag)
;      Adds enrichment multiplier based on load change rate (g/rev/cycle)
;   3. During tip-OUT (throttle closing):
;      Tip-in: INACTIVE (only responds to rising throttle)
;      Tau falling load: ACTIVE (prevents rich spike on decel)
;
;   Both systems give MORE enrichment when engine is COLD:
;     Tip-in ECT B: +250% at -40F, tapering to 0% at 140F+
;     Tau Rising (1.75 g/r): 3.40x at -40F, tapering to 0.32x at 176F+
;
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; SUBSYSTEM 1: TIP-IN ENRICHMENT (Throttle-Rate Based)
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
;
; Trigger:  delta(throttle_angle) per cycle
; Output:   Additional Injector Pulse Width (ms) added to base IPW
; Purpose:  Compensate for intake manifold fuel film lag on sudden throttle
;           opening — prevents lean stumble during tip-in transients.
; Code:     fuel_transient_comp @ 0x37186, fuel_accel_enrich @ 0x3BB6C
;
; ─── Primary Tables ──────────────────────────────────
;   0xCED08:  TipIn_ThrottleAngleChange_Axis  (18 float32, throttle delta %)
;   0xCED50:  TipInEnrichA                    (18 uint16, IPW adder ms, scale 0.004)
;   0xCEDBC:  TipInEnrichB                    (alternate enrichment table)
;
; ─── Compensation Tables ─────────────────────────────
;   0xCD0D8:  TipIn_RPMComp_Axis              (16 float32 RPM breakpoints)
;   0xCD118:  TipIn_RPMComp                   (16 uint8, RPM scaling: low RPM = reduced)
;   0xCD14C:  TipIn_BoostErrorComp            (boost error compensation)
;   0xCD155:  TipIn_ECTComp_A                 (ECT variant A)
;   0xCEDE0:  TipIn_ECTComp_B                 (ECT variant B, cold: +250%)
;   0xCEE00:  TipIn_ECTComp_C                 (ECT variant C)
;   0xCEE40:  TipIn_ECTComp_D                 (ECT variant D)
;
; ─── Activation & Disable Controls ───────────────────
;   0xCC4A0:  TipIn_MinThrottleActivation     (min throttle angle change to fire)
;   0xCC4A4:  TipIn_MinIPWActivation          (min IPW adder after compensations)
;   0xCBC08:  TipIn_AppliedCounterReset       (counter reset cycles)
;   0xCD165:  TipIn_DisableCounter_A          (applied counter threshold, ECT-indexed)
;   0xCD175:  TipIn_DisableCounter_B          (applied counter threshold, ECT-indexed)
;   0xCEE60:  TipIn_CumulativeThreshold_A     (cumulative throttle angle disable)
;   0xCEE80:  TipIn_CumulativeThreshold_B     (cumulative throttle angle disable)
;
; ─── Acceleration Enrichment Gains ───────────────────
;   0xCC51C:  AccelEnrich_TipInGain            (tip-in gain coefficient)
;   0xCC530:  AccelEnrich_TipOutGain           (tip-out gain coefficient)
;   0xCBC0B:  AccelEnrich_Cal_A                (accel enrich calibration A)
;   0xCBC0C:  AccelEnrich_Cal_B                (accel enrich calibration B)
;
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; SUBSYSTEM 2: TAU — ALPHA TRANSIENT FUELING (Load-Rate Based)
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
;
; Trigger:  delta(engine_load) per cycle (g/rev change rate)
; Output:   Enrichment Adder Multiplier (dimensionless, scales a base adder)
; Purpose:  Compensate for fuel film dynamics during load transients that
;           may NOT correspond to throttle changes (e.g., boost spool,
;           gear changes, altitude changes).
; Code:     Integrated into fuel_transient_comp @ 0x37186
;
; ─── Rising Load Tables (engine load INCREASING) ─────
;   0xCCDCC:  Tau_RisingLoad_Axis             (3 float32 engine load breakpoints, g/rev)
;   0xCD6E6:  Tau_RisingLoad_A                (3x16 uint16 map, load x ECT)
;             Scale: 0.00048828125. Cold=3.40x at -40F, warm=0.32x at 176F+
;             ECT axis: shared PSE CT axis @ 0xCC624 (16 bins, -40 to 110 degF)
;
; ─── Falling Load Tables (engine load DECREASING) ────
;   0xCD746:  Tau_FallingLoad                 (16 uint16, ECT-indexed)
;   0xCD766:  Tau_FallingLoad_A               (variant A)
;   0xCD848:  Tau_FallingLoad_B               (variant B)
;   0xCD868:  Tau_FallingLoad_C               (variant C)
;             Scale: 0.00048828125. Handles fuel film evaporation during
;             falling load — prevents rich spike on decel/tip-out.
;
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; SUBSYSTEM 3: OVERRUN FUEL CUTOFF (Deceleration Fuel Cut)
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
;
; Trigger:  RPM delta + airflow thresholds during deceleration
; Output:   Fuel cut (injectors off) with controlled resume enrichment
; Code:     fuel_overrun_cutoff @ 0x3EB8C, tail-calls 0x46BCC
;
; ─── Calibration Tables ──────────────────────────────
;   0xCC498:  Overrun_RPMDelta_Activation     (RPM change threshold to trigger)
;   0xCC49C:  Overrun_InitialEnrichment       (IPW adder on decel entry, ms)
;   0xCC4EC:  Overrun_FuelCut_RPMThreshold    (RPM below which fuel cut applies)
;   0xCEED0:  Overrun_FuelResume_RPMThreshold (RPM where fuel resumes after cut)
;   0xD29AA:  Overrun_Cutoff_Cal              (overrun cutoff RPM/airflow map)

; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; AVCS (VARIABLE CAM TIMING) DUTY CORRECTION TABLES
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; Reverse-engineered from ECU descriptor structures (28-byte format).
; Descriptor format: [bias(4)][dims(4)][Y_axis(4)][X_axis(4)][data(4)][storage(4)][scale(4)]
;
; ─── Intake Duty Correction A ────────────────────────
;   Descriptor @ 0xAD620 (28 bytes):
;     bias=0, dims=10x9, Y=0xCF9EC, X=0xCFA14, data=0xCFA38
;     storage=0x04000000 (uint8), scale=0x3E4CCCCC (0.2)
;
;   0xCF9EC:  VVT Error axis (Y, 10 floats): [4,6,10,15,20,25,30,40,60,80] degrees
;   0xCFA14:  RPM axis (X, 9 floats): [650,800,1000,1200,1600,2000,2400,3000,3600]
;   0xCFA38:  Data (90 uint8, 10 rows x 9 cols, physical = raw * 0.2 degrees)
;
; ─── Exhaust Duty Correction A ───────────────────────
;   Descriptor @ 0xAD848 (28 bytes):
;     bias=0, dims=10x9, Y=0xD11D0, X=0xD11F8, data=0xD121C
;     storage=0x08000000 (uint16), scale=0x38800000 (0.000061)
;
;   0xD11D0:  VVT Error axis (Y, 10 floats): [4,6,10,15,20,25,30,40,60,80] degrees
;   0xD11F8:  RPM axis (X, 9 floats): [650,800,1000,1200,1600,2000,2400,3000,3600]
;   0xD121C:  Data (90 uint16, 180 bytes, physical = raw * 0.003051758 - 100 degrees)

; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; LOW PULSE WIDTH INJECTOR COMPENSATION
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; Found via gate function (0x043470) literal pool and 0xAE000 descriptor analysis.
;
; ─── Code Functions ────────────────────────────────
;   0x043470:  LowPW_GateFunction    - Gate check: RPM < max and IPW < max
;   0x0BE874:  LowPW_TableProcessor  - Table lookup engine called by gate function
;   0x0BECA8:  LowPW_AxisLookup      - Axis lookup / interpolation helper
;
; ─── Calibration Data ──────────────────────────────
;   0xD2D20:  LowPW_GateThresh_FR8_Max  - Max FR8 gate threshold (float)
;   0xD3988:  Y axis - Base Pulse Width (8 x float32): 0.7 to 4.5 ms
;   0xD39A8:  Data - Low PW Fuel Injector Compensation (8 x uint8)
;             Scaling: InjectorPulseWidthCompensation
;   0xD2D28:  Low PW fuel injector comp maximum RPM (float)
;             Currently = 10000 RPM (feature effectively disabled)
;   0xD2D2C:  Low PW fuel injector comp maximum IPW (float)
;             Currently = 10000 raw = 10.0 ms (feature effectively disabled)

              ;   [Y Axis]  (RPM)
  000F99E0:  Requested Torque (Accelerator Pedal) SI-DRIVE Sport
              ; Drive-by-Wire Throttle (DBW)  [3D]  (Requested Torque (raw ecu value))
  000F9BE0:  Accelerator Pedal Angle
              ;   [X Axis]  (%)
  000F9C1C:  Engine Speed
              ;   [Y Axis]  (RPM)
  000F9C60:  Requested Torque (Accelerator Pedal) SI-DRIVE Sport Sharp
              ; Drive-by-Wire Throttle (DBW)  [3D]  (Requested Torque (raw ecu value))
  000F9E60:  Accelerator Pedal Angle
              ;   [X Axis]  (%)
  000F9E9C:  Engine Speed
              ;   [Y Axis]  (RPM)
  000F9EE0:  Requested Torque (Accelerator Pedal) SI-DRIVE Intelligent
              ; Drive-by-Wire Throttle (DBW)  [3D]  (Requested Torque (raw ecu value))

; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; ECU DESCRIPTOR STRUCTURES SUMMARY
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; The ECU uses fixed-format descriptor structures in ROM to reference
; calibration tables. Two formats have been identified:
;
; 28-byte descriptor (AVCS tables):
;   Offset  Size  Field
;   0x00    4     bias (additive offset, usually 0)
;   0x04    4     dimensions (rows<<16 | cols)
;   0x08    4     Y_axis pointer (float array)
;   0x0C    4     X_axis pointer (float array)
;   0x10    4     data pointer
;   0x14    4     storage type (0x04=uint8, 0x08=uint16)
;   0x18    4     scale factor (float)
;
; 20-byte descriptor (PSE tables):
;   Offset  Size  Field
;   0x00    4     meta (element count << 16 | storage type)
;   0x04    4     axis pointer (Coolant Temperature)
;   0x08    4     data pointer
;   0x0C    4     scale factor (float)
;   0x10    4     padding
;
; 12-byte descriptor (PSE Delay tables, no scale):
;   Offset  Size  Field
;   0x00    4     meta (element count << 16 | storage type)
;   0x04    4     axis pointer (Coolant Temperature)
;   0x08    4     data pointer
;
; Known descriptor regions:
;   0xAC948-0xACB3F:  PSE descriptors (26 entries)
;   0xAD620:          AVCS Intake Duty Correction A descriptor
;   0xAD848:          AVCS Exhaust Duty Correction A descriptor
;   0xAE000+:         Low PW Injector Comp descriptors (gate fn 0x043470)

; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
; ROM MEMORY MAP SUMMARY
; ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
;   0x00000000-0x00000030:  Exception vector table
;   0x00000BAC-0x00000BFC:  NMI handler + default exception handler
;   0x00000C0C-0x00000D36:  Reset / startup initialization
;   0x0000E628:             Scheduler table
;   0x00014004-0x000F9EE0:  Calibration tables (590+)
;   0x00029858:             Helper functions
;   0x00030674-0x00030A78:  Post Start Enrichment code function
;   0x00043470:             Low PW Injector Comp gate function
;   0x0008D838:             Pointer table (ptr_table_8D838, purpose TBD)
;   0x000BE874:             LowPW_TableProcessor (table lookup engine)
;   0x000BECA8:             LowPW_AxisLookup (interpolation helper)
;   0x00043750-0x00043B62:  Knock detection (wrapper + detector)
;   0x00045BFE-0x00045DD8:  FLKC Path J (fast knock correction)
;   0x000463BA-0x000466A0:  FLKC Paths F/G (sustained knock correction)
;   0x0004A94C:             Scheduler periodic dispatch
;   0x0004AD40-0x0004AE2C:  59-entry periodic task table
;   0x0009A770-0x0009A82B:  Diagnostic Trouble Codes (DTCs)
;   0x000AC948-0x000ACB3F:  PSE descriptor table (26 entries)
;   0x000AD620:             AVCS Intake descriptor
;   0x000AD848:             AVCS Exhaust descriptor
;   0x000AE000+:            Low PW Injector Comp descriptors
;   0x000C0000-0x000FFFFF:  Primary calibration data region
;     0x000C009E:            Wastegate Duty Cycle Frequency
;     0x000C0BC8:            Boost disable during fuel cut (tiny wrex patch)
;     0x000D29AC-0x000D29B3:  Map Switching cruise switch counters (4 x uint16)
;     0x000D2A08-0x000D2ABC:  Map Switching cruise/non-cruise thresholds (37 params)
;     0x000D2AE8-0x000D2B1C:  Timing Blend parameters (14 params)
;     0x000F104C-0x000F1054:  tiny wrex patches (LC speed, LC RPM delta, FFS RPM delta)
;   0xFFFF8000-0xFFFFFFFF:  Internal RAM (32KB)



================================================================================
AFC / CLOSED-LOOP FUEL FEEDBACK SYSTEM — COMPLETE TRACE
================================================================================
ROM: AE5L600L (2013 USDM Impreza WRX MT)  |  MCU: SH7058 SH-2 BE
Analysis: Ghidra 12.0.2 + binary cross-reference tracing
================================================================================

EXECUTIVE SUMMARY
=================
There is NO single table or function called "AFC" in this ECU. The Subaru
closed-loop fuel system is decomposed into 5 subsystems:

  1. CL/OL State Machine    — Decides when to run closed-loop vs open-loop
  2. Front O2 Sensor Input   — Wideband lambda sensor reading → AFR
  3. Short-Term Correction    — Real-time AFC adjustment (not yet labeled in Ghidra)
  4. A/F Learning (LTFT)      — Long-term fuel trim stored in 4 airflow ranges
  5. AF 3 Correction          — Rear O2 trim (DISABLED in this ROM — limits = 0%)

The code lives in ROM 0x33000-0x37000 and is dispatched from two secondary
task tables (NOT the 59-entry periodic scheduler used by knock/FLKC).


================================================================================
SECTION 1: DISPATCH — HOW THE FUELING CODE GETS CALLED
================================================================================

The fueling functions are invoked from two dispatch tables in the scheduler
region, separate from the 59-task periodic table @ 0x4AD40:

  DISPATCH TABLE A @ 0x480B8 (8 fueling entries):
  ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  0x480B8: -> 0x33278   Main fueling pre-calc
  0x480CC: -> 0x34488   A/F Learning sub-dispatcher
  0x480D0: -> 0x357D0   CL/OL transition sub B
  0x480D4: -> 0x34EC8   A/F Learning airflow range processor
  0x480D8: -> 0x36008   CL/OL delay manager A
  0x480DC: -> 0x36A98   CL/OL hysteresis handler
  0x480E0: -> 0x36BF4   CL/OL delay manager B
  0x480E4: -> 0x36E60   Post-transition handler

  DISPATCH TABLE B @ 0x4A0B8 (6 fueling entries):
  ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  0x4A0B8: -> 0x332A2   Main fueling entry (NON-RETURNING)
  0x4A0E0: -> 0x36C3C   OL/CL state cleanup
  0x4A0E8: -> 0x3452A   A/F Learning core (refs CC064)
  0x4A0EC: -> 0x34EF4   A/F Learning airflow update
  0x4A0F0: -> 0x3580C   CL/OL transition core
  0x4A0F4: -> 0x3605E   OL fuel map selector (refs CC16C)

  The main fueling entry at 0x332A2 is flagged as "non-returning" by Ghidra,
  suggesting it's a persistent loop or state machine rather than a one-shot task.


================================================================================
SECTION 2: CL/OL STATE MACHINE — WHEN DOES AFC RUN?
================================================================================

AFC (closed-loop correction) only runs when the ECU is in Closed Loop (CL) mode.
The CL/OL transition is a multi-condition state machine controlled by ~15
calibration tables. The transition logic occupies ROM 0x35100-0x36C00.

─── CL → OL Transition (AFC gets disabled) ───────────────────────────────

The ECU transitions from CL to OL when ANY of these conditions clears the
CL delay counter to zero:

  CONDITION                          TABLE ADDRESS    VALUE IN THIS ROM
  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  RPM >= Max (Per Gear)              0xCC180          3200-3700 RPM (gear-dep.)
  RPM >= Max (Neutral)               0xCC1A8          6000-6100 RPM
  Throttle >= Max                    0xCC1D8          37.9 / 90.0 deg
  Vehicle Speed >= Max               0xCC1F4          141.7 / 144.9 km/h
  Engine Load >= Max                 0xCC204          0.95 / 1.10 g/rev
  ECT < Minimum                      0xCC17C          -12.0 °F

  CRITICAL: CL to OL Delay @ 0xCBC62 = 0.0
  ──────────────────────────────────────────
  The base CL→OL delay counter is SET TO ZERO in this ROM.
  This means there is NO delay — the transition to OL is IMMEDIATE when
  any throttle or BPW threshold is exceeded. The SI-DRIVE Intelligent
  delay (0xCBC5C) is also 0.0.

  When the delay IS non-zero, the transition uses:
    - Throttle threshold:  CL→OL Transition with Delay (Throttle) @ 0xCCD78
    - BPW threshold:       CL→OL Transition with Delay (BPW) @ 0xCE5F8
    - Counter increment:   CL→OL Counter Step Value (MAF) @ 0xCE640

  The counter increments each cycle that throttle OR BPW exceeds the threshold.
  When counter >= delay value, transition occurs.

─── OL → CL Transition (AFC gets re-enabled) ─────────────────────────────

  The ECU returns to CL when:
    Throttle <= (CL→OL Throttle Threshold - Hysteresis)
    AND
    BPW <= (CL→OL BPW Threshold - BPW Hysteresis)

  Hysteresis values:
    Throttle hysteresis:  8.4 deg  (0xCC178)
    BPW hysteresis:       756.0    (0xCC174)

  NOTE: The large BPW hysteresis (756) means the ECU requires a significant
  drop in fuel demand before returning to CL mode.

─── Code Structure ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  Literal pool clusters in the CL/OL transition code:

  0x35120-0x351D8 (46 entries) — Initial CL/OL check
    Reads: RPM (FFFF6350), MAF (FFFF6624), ECT (FFFF63CC),
           Gear (FFFF5E94), Vehicle Speed
    Refs:  CC0AC-CC0D0 calibration, multiple table processor calls

  0x36278-0x362F8 (31 entries) — OL fuel map switch (IAM check)
    Key ref: 0xCC16C (IAM threshold = 0.5)
    Reads:  IAM value (FFFF3234), RPM, MAF
    Calls:  0x22F92 (utility function)
    Logic:  If IAM < 0.5 → switch to failsafe fuel maps

  0x36534-0x365D8 (41 entries) — Per-gear RPM limit check
    Refs:  CC180-CC1D4 (all 10 per-gear RPM thresholds)
    Reads: Current gear (FFFF5E94/5E92/5E93/5DB5)
    Logic: If RPM >= threshold for current gear → clear CL delay → OL

  0x367B8-0x36824 (27 entries) — Multi-condition CL delay clear
    Refs:  CC1A8 (Neutral RPM), CC1D8 (Throttle max), CC1F4 (Speed max),
           CC204 (Load max), CC17C (ECT min), CBC5A (Load counter thresh),
           CBC5C/CBC62 (CL/OL delay values), CBC60/CBC64
    Logic: Checks each condition sequentially, clears delay if exceeded

  0x36A0C-0x36A98 (33 entries) — Hysteresis and OL entry confirmation
    Refs:  CC178 (Throttle hysteresis), CC174 (BPW hysteresis)
    Reads: FFFF798C, FFFF79F8 (current throttle/BPW state)
    Logic: Applies hysteresis to prevent CL/OL oscillation


================================================================================
SECTION 3: FRONT O2 SENSOR — THE FEEDBACK INPUT
================================================================================

The front O2 sensor is a WIDEBAND (air/fuel ratio) sensor, not a narrowband
switching sensor. It reads pump current in milliamps and converts to AFR.

─── Sensor Scaling Table @ 0xD8DA8 (Y-axis @ 0xD8D74) ───────────────────

  Sensor Current (mA)   →   Lambda    →    AFR
  ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  -1.300 mA             →   0.7586    →   11.15
  -0.870 mA             →   0.8276    →   12.17
  -0.470 mA             →   0.8966    →   13.18
  -0.140 mA             →   0.9655    →   14.19
   0.000 mA             →   1.0000    →   14.70  ← stoichiometric
   0.100 mA             →   1.0345    →   15.21
   0.240 mA             →   1.1034    →   16.22
   0.390 mA             →   1.1724    →   17.23
   0.530 mA             →   1.2414    →   18.25
   0.640 mA             →   1.3103    →   19.26
   0.740 mA             →   1.3793    →   20.28

  Rich limit:   AFR 11.02 (lambda 0.750) @ 0x21CAC
  Lean limit:   AFR 29.40 (lambda 2.000) — hardcoded in compensation formula

  Atmospheric compensation @ 0xC3708:
    Formula: ((Front O2 AFR - 14.7) × Compensation) + 14.7
    The compensation value adjusts for altitude/barometric pressure.

  Front AF Sensor Smoothing (Alpha category):
    A 4×4 table indexed by Smoothed MAF × Engine Load.
    WARNING: "DO NOT SET TO 100% or higher!"
    Lower values = less smoothing = faster response.
    This smoothing factor directly affects how quickly AFC can respond.

─── Sensor Processing Path (Code Functions) ───────────────────────────────

  0x004A2C:  frontO2_scaling_init
             Initializes/reads front O2 sensor scaling via descriptor @ 0xAF45C.

  0x058902:  frontO2_scaling_lookup
             Performs the 2D interpolation through the scaling table.
             Accesses descriptor @ 0xAF468 (Y-axis at D8D74, data at D8DA8).

  0x021A40:  frontO2_process (MAIN O2 PROCESSING FUNCTION)
             - Loads rich limit (lambda 0.750) from inline literal pool at 0x21CAC
               via mova @(0x230,PC),R0 + fmov.s @R0,FR12
             - Accesses atmospheric compensation descriptor @ 0xAAE8C
             - Applies formula: ((AFR - 14.7) × compensation) + 14.7
             - Clamps result to rich limit

  0x01FE54:  frontO2_comp_atm
             Atmospheric pressure compensation sub-function.
             Accesses descriptor @ 0xAAE78.

  Processing pipeline:
  1. ADC reads wideband sensor pump current → raw mA value
  2. frontO2_scaling_init (0x4A2C) → initializes scaling
  3. frontO2_scaling_lookup (0x58902) → 2D interpolation → lambda value
  4. frontO2_process (0x21A40) → rich limit clamp + atm compensation
  5. Smoothing filter applied (Alpha table)
  6. Result stored in RAM for AFC feedback loop


================================================================================
SECTION 4: A/F LEARNING — LONG-TERM FUEL TRIM (LTFT)
================================================================================

The A/F Learning system stores long-term corrections in 4 airflow ranges.
Code is at ROM 0x34490-0x34EC8, dispatched from 0x4A0E8 (entry: 0x3452A).

─── Calibration Data ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  A/F Learning #1 Limits @ 0xCC064:
    Minimum: -0.250 (= -25%)
    Maximum: +0.250 (= +25%)

  A/F Learning #1 Airflow Ranges @ 0xCC074:
    Range A:  6.0 - 23.0 g/s    (idle / light cruise)
    Range B: 40.0 - 80.0 g/s    (moderate load)
    Range C:  0.95 - 1.05 g/s   (deceleration / very low flow)
    Range D: 35.0 -  0.0 g/s    (DISABLED — max < min)

  A/F #1 Learning Max Threshold (Alpha): Controls the maximum MAF where
    learning values are applied. Setting below D range prevents fuel
    learnings from carrying into open loop fueling.

  A/F #1 Learning Min Threshold (Alpha): Controls minimum MAF for learning.

─── Code Analysis ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  Entry point: 0x3452A (called from dispatch table B @ 0x4A0E8)

  Function structure (traced from disassembly):

  0x3452A: Main A/F Learning entry
    Saves r9, r13, r14, PR
    Calls:
      0x34D52  — Subroutine (purpose TBD, appears to be precondition check)
      0x345A4  — CL Active Check (see below)
      0x34778  — Subroutine (learning range selection?)
      0x34884  — Subroutine (learning value update?)
      0x34B1C  — Subroutine (learning value storage?)
      0x34CC8  — Post-processing
      0x34C18  — Cleanup
    Reads RAM: FFFF7D68 (float), FFFF78A4 (output area)
    Writes: FFFF78A0 region (A/F learning output data structure)

  0x345A4: CL Active Check function
    This function checks 8 conditions to determine if CL is active.
    Returns 1 (CL active, learning OK) or 0 (not active, skip learning).

    Conditions checked (all must pass for CL active):
      1. RAM[FFFF8F24] — Global enable flag
      2. Comparison vs calibration @ 0xCC020 (= 70.0) — likely MAF threshold
         FFFF78A0[-20] (float) must be <= 70.0 g/s
      3. RAM[FFFF73A4] — via BE608 table processor check
      4. RAM[FFFF7354] — via BE608 table processor check
      5. RAM[FFFF7374] — via BE608 table processor check
      6. RAM[FFFF7A14] — via BE608 table processor check
      7. RAM[FFFF7A20] — via BE608 table processor check
      8. RAM[FFFF7D18] — Scheduler status (also used by FLKC)
      9. r14 (FFFF8F24 flag again)
     10. RAM[FFFF7BE2] — Final enable check

    If ANY check fails → return 0 → skip A/F learning update
    Result stored at FFFF78A0+3 (byte flag: CL learning active)

  0x344BA: A/F Learning loop (4 iterations)
    Iterates over 4 airflow ranges (r12 = 4, counter in r14)
    For each range:
      - Loads float from FFFF316C + offset (learning table base in RAM)
      - Calls 0xBDBCC (likely a table interpolation/update function)
      - Passes current learning value as fr14 parameter
      - Updates at 8-byte intervals (float value + metadata per range)

  0x344EE: Range validity check (4 iterations)
    Same loop structure, calls 0xBDCB6 for each range
    If ANY range returns non-zero → sets flag (r12 = 1)
    This checks if learning values are within valid limits

─── RAM Variables (A/F Learning) ──────────────────────────────────────────

  0xFFFF316C:  A/F Learning table base in RAM (4 ranges × 8 bytes)
  0xFFFF78A0:  A/F Learning output data structure (large, ~100 bytes)
    +0x03:     CL active flag (byte, set by 0x345A4)
    +0xD8(-40): Learning output value (float, written at 0x344B0)
    +0xE4(-28): RPM snapshot (float)
    +0xE8(-24): Load snapshot (float)
    +0xEC(-20): AFR snapshot (float)
    +0xF0(-16): Additional snapshot
  0xFFFF78A4:  Learning output secondary area
  0xFFFF7874:  Learning state flags
  0xFFFF787F:  Current airflow range index (byte, 0-3)
  0xFFFF8F24:  Global CL enable flag

─── Key Literal Pool @ 0x34678 (38 entries) ───────────────────────────────

  RAM variables:  FFFF6254, FFFF78A0, FFFF316C, FFFF787F, FFFF6350,
                  FFFF78A4, FFFF6364, FFFF63FC, FFFF69FC, FFFF6A22,
                  FFFF7D68, FFFF8F24, FFFF7324, FFFF733C, FFFF7448,
                  FFFF94B1, FFFF7453, FFFFA56A, FFFFACE6
  Calibration:    CC068 (AFL max), CC064 (AFL min), CC020 (MAF thresh)
  Code calls:     022F92, 063A5C, 029BA4, 0BE56C, 0BDBCC, 0BDCB6, 0BE608


================================================================================
SECTION 5: AF 3 CORRECTION — REAR O2 TRIM (DISABLED)
================================================================================

  AF 3 Correction Limits @ 0x35FFC:
    Minimum: 0.000000 → 0.00%
    Maximum: 0.000000 → 0.00%

  BOTH LIMITS ARE ZERO. The rear O2 sensor has NO influence on fuel trim
  in this ROM. Per the XML definition:

    "CHANGING THIS VALUE MIN-MAX TO 0 INPUT RESULTS IN THE DISABLITY
     OF THE REAR O2 SENSOR INPUT ON TARGET AFR. THIS AFR TRIM 3 CAN
     CAUSE RICHER THAT DISIRED IDLES WHEN LEFT ON. DISABLE IF
     EXPERINCING RICHER THAN IDEAL IDLES."

  This is an intentional tune choice, not a defect.


================================================================================
SECTION 6: CL FUELING TARGET — WHAT AFR DOES CL AIM FOR?
================================================================================

The CL fueling target is 14.7 AFR (stoichiometric) adjusted by compensation
tables based on engine load and coolant temperature.

─── Compensation Tables ───────────────────────────────────────────────────

  CL Fueling Target Comp A (Load) @ 0xD14D0:
    3D table (RPM × Load → AFR additive adjustment)
    Typical values: -0.01 to -0.61 AFR
    At high load: up to -0.61 AFR (target = 14.09)
    At low load:  -0.01 AFR (target ≈ 14.69)

  CL Fueling Target Comp B (Load) @ 0xD1740:
    Same format, alternate calibration

  CL Fueling Target Comp Imm. Cruise (ECT) @ 0xD13B0:
    Coolant temperature compensation during cruise

  CL Fueling Target Comp Imm. Non-Cruise (ECT) @ 0xD141C:
    Coolant temperature compensation during non-cruise

  CL Fueling Target Comp (ECT) Disable @ 0xCBF9C:
    Threshold: 119.0 °F
    Above this coolant temp, ECT compensation is no longer applied.

  NOTE from XML: "Lean compensation in this table will potentially force
  open loop during normally closed loop fueling conditions."


================================================================================
SECTION 7: OL FUEL MAP SELECTION — THE FAILSAFE PATH
================================================================================

When the ECU is in Open Loop, fuel is determined by lookup tables rather
than O2 sensor feedback. Map selection depends on IAM (Ignition Advance
Multiplier):

  Primary OL Fuel Map Switch (IAM) @ 0xCC16C: threshold = 0.500

  IAM >= 0.500:  Normal maps (KCA Low @ D0244, KCA High @ D0404,
                              KCA Alternate @ CFD30)
                 Max raw = 0x2B (43) → minimum AFR = 11.00

  IAM < 0.500:   Begin failsafe transition
  IAM < 0.050:   Full failsafe

  Failsafe Map @ 0xD05C4:
    Max raw = 0x46 (70) → minimum AFR = 9.50
    At 2000 RPM / 2.60 g/rev: raw=0x3C (60)
      AFR = 14.7 / (1 + 60 × 0.0078125) = 14.7 / 1.46875 = 10.02
    THIS IS THE ROOT CAUSE OF THE OBSERVED "10.02 AFR Final Fueling Base"

  Minimum Active Primary OL Enrichment @ 0xCC170: 0.050 (5%)
    Ensures at least 5% enrichment when in OL mode.

  Code at 0x3605E (dispatched from 0x4A0F4):
    Reads IAM from RAM[FFFF3234]
    Compares against threshold at CC16C
    Selects appropriate fuel map set
    Multiple descriptor pointers at AD674, AD690, AD6AC, AD6C8, AD6E4, AD700
    point to the various OL fuel map descriptors


================================================================================
SECTION 8: THE SHORT-TERM FUEL TRIM / AFC MECHANISM — FULLY TRACED
================================================================================

The AFC (short-term fuel correction) has been traced at the instruction level.
It is called from the CL fueling dispatcher at 0x33304, which sequences
through a chain of BSR calls to process the complete CL correction pipeline.

─── AFC Dispatcher: Function 0x33304 ───────────────────────────────────────

  This function is the CL fueling master controller. After checking
  CL enable conditions (RAM 0xFFFF65F0, 0xCBBD8-0xCBBDB), it calls:

  1. BSR 0x33D1C  — cl_fuel_target_B    (CL Fueling Target Comp B/Load)
  2. BSR 0x33CC0  — cl_fuel_target_A    (CL Fueling Target Comp A/Load)
  3. BSR 0x33658  — afc_sensor_prep     (sensor state & conditioning)
  4. BSR 0x33FCE  — afc_target_calc     (target computation w/ compensation)
  5. BSR 0x340A0  — afc_correction_acc  (correction factor accumulator)
  6. BSR 0x342A8  — afc_pi_controller   (THE AFC PI LOOP)
  7. JSR 0x3439E  — afc_enable_gate     (AFC enable/disable check)
  8. JSR 0x343CE  — afc_output_clamp    (AFC output limiter)

  Arguments are passed via R4/R5 pointers into a RAM variable address
  table at 0x63A2C-0x63A70 which maps correction slots:
    0x63A2C → 0xFFFF77C8  (CL correction state — widely consumed)
    0x63A3C → 0xFFFF782A  (AFC intermediate value)
    0x63A40 → 0xFFFF7864  (AFC correction output)
    0x63A44 → 0xFFFF77DC  (CL target comp A output)
    0x63A48 → 0xFFFF77E0  (CL target comp B output)

─── AFC PI Controller: Function 0x342A8 ────────────────────────────────────

  This is the core short-term correction loop. Disassembly reveals:

  RAM variables read:
    0xFFFF77C8  — Current CL correction state (accumulated)
    0xFFFF6540  — Sensor state variable
    0xFFFF7448  — CL/OL mode flag (shared with learning + scheduler)

  Operations (from disassembly):
    1. Load current correction state from 0xFFFF77C8
    2. Branch based on CL conditions (bf/s at 0x342C2, 0x342CA, 0x342D4)
    3. Compute error: fsub FR8,FR4 (actual - target) at 0x342DA
    4. Look up P gain: jsr 0xBEAB0 (table lookup) at 0x342E0
    5. Compare vs limit: fcmp/gt FR0,FR8 from ROM 0xCC000 (=2.0)
    6. Conditional clamp at ROM 0xCC004 (=20.0 max %)
    7. Store intermediate to RAM 0xFFFF7864 at multiple branch paths
    8. Second error path: fadd FR8,FR4 at 0x34374 (reverse direction)
    9. Second gain lookup: jsr 0xBE970 at 0x34378
    10. Compare vs ROM 0xCC008 (=0.0) and 0xCC00C (=1.0)
    11. Final store to RAM 0xFFFF7864

  The function has 6 distinct branch paths writing to 0xFFFF7864,
  handling: lean error, rich error, limit clamping, and enable/disable.

─── AFC Calibration Constants (UNDOCUMENTED — not in XML) ──────────────────

  ROM Address   Float Value   Purpose
  ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  0xCC000       2.0           AFC P gain / step size
  0xCC004       20.0          AFC max correction limit (%)
  0xCC008       0.0           AFC min correction or dead band
  0xCC00C       1.0           AFC I gain / unity scale factor
  0xCC010       0.0           AFC enable threshold (gate, in 0x3439E)
  0xCC014       200.0         AFC output upper clamp (in 0x343CE)
  0xCC018       190.0         AFC output lower clamp
  0xCC01C       0.0           Additional limit / reserved

─── AFC Enable Gate: Function 0x3439E ──────────────────────────────────────

  Short function. Calls 0x2BE2C and 0x2BE38 (utility checks).
  Reads ROM 0xCC010 (=0.0). This gates whether the AFC correction
  is applied. When conditions aren't met, AFC output is zeroed.

─── AFC Output Clamp: Function 0x343CE ─────────────────────────────────────

  Reads output from RAM 0xFFFF7820, applies:
    - Upper clamp from ROM 0xCC014 (=200.0%)
    - Lower clamp from ROM 0xCC018 (=190.0%)
    - Additional logic from ROM 0xCC01C (=0.0)
  Stores final clamped AFC back to RAM 0xFFFF7820.

  Also reads 0xFFFF64D8, 0xFFFF79C2, 0xFFFF79C4.

─── CL/OL AFC Decision & Hysteresis: Function 0x033DBE ─────────────────────

  This function decides whether AFC runs. Sets GBR = 0xFFFF77F4.
  Calls 0x22F92 for CL enable check. When CL is active, it looks up
  a correction from table descriptor 0xACE8C and stores to 0xFFFF77F4.
  When CL is inactive, it writes 0.0 (AFC disabled).

  Hysteresis thresholds at ROM 0xCBFD0-0xCBFE4 control the switching
  between CL active/inactive states to prevent oscillation.

─── AFC PI Output Stage: Function 0x340A0 ──────────────────────────────────

  This is the PI controller output stage with full P and I gain
  table lookups. It computes the blended PI correction:

  PROPORTIONAL path:
    P_gain_A = table lookup from 0xACEA0 (indexed by load)
    P_gain_B = table lookup from 0xACEB4 (indexed by RPM)
    P_norm   = table lookup from 0xAC4FC (indexed by airflow)
    proportional = (P_gain_A + P_gain_B) * P_norm

  INTEGRAL path:
    I_comp   = 2D table from 0xAD928 (indexed by coolant × AFR)
    I_gain_A = table lookup from 0xACEC8 (indexed by load)
    I_gain_B = table lookup from 0xACEDC (indexed by RPM)
    I_norm   = table lookup from 0xAC510 (indexed by airflow)
    integral = (I_comp + I_gain_A + I_gain_B) * I_norm

  BLEND (classic PI):
    output = proportional * alpha + integral * (1 - alpha)

  Reads flags at: 0xFFFF8E7E, 0xFFFF85D7
  Outputs to: 0xFFFF7870, and via subroutine bsr 0x33A0E

─── Where AFC Feeds Into IPW ───────────────────────────────────────────────

  The AFC correction value in RAM 0xFFFF77C8 is consumed by the
  fuel correction accumulator function at 0x320AE. This function:

  Reads:
    0xFFFF77C8  — AFC/CL correction (from the PI controller)
    0xFFFF7820  — AFC output (clamped value)
    0xFFFF77D8  — Additional correction factor
    0xFFFF781C  — Additional correction factor
    0xFFFF77E4  — Additional correction factor
    0xFFFF77DC  — CL target comp A output
    0xFFFF7448  — Mode flag
    0xFFFF7714  — IPW-related variable
    0xFFFF7710  — IPW-related variable

  Performs table lookups via 0xBE608, 0xBE628, 0xBE970, 0xBE5A8
  to combine all correction factors (AFC, LTFT, enrichments, etc.)
  into the final injector pulse width multiplier.

  This is the final stage where:
    Final IPW = Base IPW × (1 + AFC) × (1 + LTFT) × other corrections

─── Why AFC and AFL are zero during OL→CL transitions ────────────────────

  Now confirmed by code trace:

  a) CL→OL is IMMEDIATE (delay = 0 in this ROM, see 0xCBC62)
  b) During OL, the AFC dispatcher (0x33304) does NOT execute the
     PI controller — the BSR chain is gated by the CL enable check
  c) AFC output (0xFFFF7864) is zeroed or frozen during OL
  d) On return to CL, the PI controller restarts from the current
     state — likely near zero if OL was long enough
  e) The front O2 sensor smoothing adds additional lag
  f) If the transition is brief (bouncing at the threshold), AFC
     never has time to build up a meaningful correction

  The A/F Learning Max Threshold (Alpha table) controls whether LTFT
  carries into OL. If set below the D range airflow, learnings are
  completely excluded from OL fueling — the OL maps run "raw."
